# Set the FT_PREFIX environment variable to the value of stage.variables.application_functional_tests_input if it starts with "mvn", otherwise use the DEFAULT_PREFIX
FT_PREFIX=${DEFAULT_PREFIX}

# Set the FT_SUFFIX environment variable to a default Maven command suffix with placeholders replaced by pipeline variables
FT_SUFFIX="$SETTINGS_PATH"

# Set the FULL_CMD environment variable to the concatenation of FT_PREFIX and FT_SUFFIX
FULL_CMD="${FT_PREFIX} ${FT_SUFFIX}"

IFS=';' read -ra cmds <<< "$FULL_CMD"
CNT=0
FT_TDP_RUN_URLS=""
for cmd in "${cmds[@]}"; do
    # Print the value of FULL_CMD
    echo "${cmd}"

    # Execute the command stored in FULL_CMD
    ${cmd} 2>&1 | tee -a ft_log_$CNT.out

    command_exit_status=${PIPESTATUS[0]}

    # Finding FT TDP runid URL
    TDP_RUN_URL=`cat ft_log_$CNT.out | grep 'testRunID:https://engineering.paypalcorp.com/console/ext/test-data-platform/testrun?id=' | grep -oE "https?://[^ ]+" | sort -u`
    if [[ $TDP_RUN_URL =~ "https://engineering.paypalcorp.com/console/ext/test-data-platform/testrun?id=" ]]; then
        if [[ $CNT -gt 0 ]]; then
            FT_TDP_RUN_URLS="$FT_TDP_RUN_URLS,$TDP_RUN_URL"
        else
            FT_TDP_RUN_URLS="$TDP_RUN_URL"
        fi
        echo "INFO: FT tdp run urls - $FT_TDP_RUN_URLS"
        if [[ -z $FT_TDP_RUN_URLS || $FT_TDP_RUN_URLS == null || $FT_TDP_RUN_URLS == "" ]]; then
            FT_TDP_RUN_URLS="INFO: PLease onboard your application onto TDP."
        fi
    fi
    if [ "$command_exit_status" -ne 0 ]; then
        echo "INFO: Command failed with exit status $command_exit_status. Exiting."
        exit "$command_exit_status"
    fi
    CNT=$((CNT + 1))
done

deploystatus=`cat cmsdb.json | jq '.result[].lastSuccessfulDeploymentTime'`
if [[ -z $deploystatus || $deploystatus == null || $deploystatus == "" ]]; then
    echo "ERROR: Deployment is not successfully registered with CMS DB."
